100682557079571885286</user>
<Time>1567054200666< /Time>< review>
Have shopped at Smart & Final for a long time. Clean stores, most have a good selection of product, produce is fresh, well maintained and generally of very good quality. Same with the meats and frozen goods. However their home brand goods and name brand goods I feel are on the high side. Now their sale goods sometimes are quite a good deal, for instance today I purchased California raised and butchered chicken half breasts, bone in for $0.88 a pound. Now I won't mention the farm that it came from but they are always fresh, always in CA. That's just about half price! Whenever I see a good price for something I like and use it's usually at S&F. But tonight I broke my Cardinal rule for grocery shopping, don't shop hungry, lol!</review>

< username>
Stacey King<//username>
<date>1511981012619</date><rating>4<//rating>< Text>
Four and a half stars for a very charming B&B experience. Location was close to downtown, but not close enough to walk. Uber was our friend here. Loved the place however. Felt very much like I was visiting family. The owner is a very sweet woman who genuinely wants each guest to have a good experience in her home and in Sonoma. Our room was cozy. I wouldn't call it luxurious but it was very comfortable and cute. The bathroom was huge. There was a jetted tub and large vanity. Local boutique brand shampoos and soaps were a nice touch. Breakfast was superb!! Delicious and filling and beautifully presented. We enjoyed meeting and interacting with the other guests and it was overall, a wonderful B&B experience. My only recommendation is for those who may not be early risers or are sensitive to noise:  be sure to request one of the upstairs rooms. We were in the downstairs room, just off the kitchen. The door is glass and did not feel completely private (there was only a thin window covering and it wasn't totally adequate), and the noise of morning coffee and meal preparations awoke us each day. While it wasn't a bother for us, it may not be for those who wish to sleep in.

This place is a terrific value and I highly recommend it to Sonoma Valley visitors.< /Text>

<time>1438967160271<//time><pictures>None< /pictures>< Text>
This was a beautiful B&B located right off the main drag in Sonoma.  The staff was friendly and the room was very cozy.  The inn gives you a card which gives you free tastings at wineries/tasting rooms.  It says on the card "complimentary wine tasting" but don't be deceived into thinking its completely free tastings for you and your spouse/girlfriend.  We were informed at the first tasting room that the card actually gives you a BOGO on tastings, which is still a good deal since most of the tastings range from $10-$20 per person.  The only disappoint for me was breakfast.  Though it was quite delicious it was very small both mornings we were there.  The first morning we had the inn's take on eggs benedict.  Normally when you order eggs benedict at a restaurant you get two english muffins with all the ingredients on top.  At Cinnamon Bear we were given just one with a side of cantaloupe, which neither my wife or I like.  There were no other options or sides so my wife and I actually went to the bakery in the plaza to supplement our breakfast.  The second day we were given two smaller-sized pancakes, some ham mixed with some type of fruit, and the cantaloupe again.  Other than the breakfast this place certainly is worth staying at, especially for the price.<//Text>

<rate>5</rate>< text>
We lucked out and got a booking at the last minute due to a cencellation.

THIS PLACE IS FANTASTIC!  We booked a king suite and arrived a bit early so we got to pick the downstairs master room.  It included a heater, a fireplace, an airconditioner/ionizer and a shower with great water pressure.  The bed was very comfortable and the room was quiet even being located on the street level (fence with garden between room and road).

There is a concrete patio creekside for lounging as well as a nice living room with fireplace in the building.

The daily breakfast is great but it isn't served until 8:30.  WIFI is available but it was a bit slow.

The receptionist was super nice and friendly and we felt welcome like going to grandma's house.

The location is convenient to the downtown square as well as the wineries n Sonoma Hwy (go north for fabulous scenery and wine tastings).  The Inn will give you a card for free tastings at 30 wineries...use it.

Whe we come back to Sonoma, we will definitely stqy here.< /text>

<Name>Sean Shih</Name><time>1577249275954< /time><Rating>5</Rating>< Text>
THIS PLACE IS RECOMMENDED.

Tried out this place after a disappointing first time visit at the other near-by Hot Pot restaurant, hands down Pot On Fire is clearly a much better choice in the Chino Hills area.

What make it stand out is the vast choices of soup base, the meat is lean, nicely trimmed, the portion is satisfying, unlike the other place I long for more even with another side order of meat. I ordered the Sukiyaki Pot, it was very tasty.

The staffs were friendly, service was prompt and attentive, and the price is fair. I will be a return customer for sure.< /Text>

< text>
What a great experience! Went with my family and in law's for a birthday dinner. First impressions as I went in was how clean the restaurant is. Even the overhead cooking hoods were spotless, not a drop of grease present anywhere.  The whole place was spotless.  The menu is simple and straightforward with plenty of variety.  We ordered some apps while we waited for the show.

Mack came to the grill and started his show with fire. He did a great job with a lot of skill and humor. His cooking was well executed and the food tasted great. Even my very picky son liked the chicken teriyaki, a dish he had to date refused to try.  I will be asking for him the next time I am there.
The prices are very reasonable, the service excellent. If you are looking for a fun experience in Elk Grove stop by.</text>
